‚óŹ Justfile added with these recipes:

  - just deps ‚ÄĒ install Python + frontend dependencies
  - just run ‚ÄĒ build frontend then start server
  - just build / just dev ‚ÄĒ frontend build / HMR dev server
  - just test ‚ÄĒ run pytest
  - just check / just fix ‚ÄĒ lint & format
  - just config <callsign> ‚ÄĒ set your callsign
  - just config-grid <grid> ‚ÄĒ set your grid square
  - just config-show ‚ÄĒ show current settings

‚ĚĮ please read CLAUDE.md my collaborator duane added some changes. Please

‚óŹ Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

‚óŹ Duane's changes:

  1. freq is now user-editable ‚ÄĒ changed from "not user-editable" to
  "auto-filled from flrig, and user-editable". Users can override the flrig
  value.
  2. skcc no longer marked optional ‚ÄĒ was "SKCC member number (optional)", now
  just "SKCC member number".
  3. New "Required Fields" section ‚ÄĒ explicitly lists call, freq, mode, and
  timestamp as required.
  4. Updated architecture note on flrig ‚ÄĒ clarifies that when flrig isn't
  running, freq/mode can be manually entered, and users can override
  flrig-supplied data.

      76 +    }

‚óŹ Bash(git add src/rigbook/flrig.py && git commit -m "run flrig XMLRPC calls in
      executor to avoid blocking async event loop" && git push)
  ‚éŅ ¬†[master 62189df] run flrig XMLRPC calls in executor to avoid blocking
     async event loop
      1 file changed, 9 insertions(+), 5 deletions(-)
     ‚Ä¶ +2 lines (ctrl+o to expand)

‚óŹ The flrig XMLRPC calls were synchronous and blocking the async event loop ‚ÄĒ
  when flrig was slow or the connection timed out, it would freeze the entire
  server and stop all polling. Now they run in a thread executor so the event
  loop stays responsive. Restart the server and it should poll properly again.

  while they're blocking in the executor, new poll requests queue up. Let me add
   a timeout:
